<p><b>Toni Kroos</b> (<small>German pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Standard_German" title="Help:IPA/Standard German">[toni kos]</a></span>; born 4 January 1990) is a German professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> club <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany national team</a>. Kroos plays mainly as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>, but has also been deployed as a <a href="/wiki/Playmaker#Deep-lying_playmakers" title="Playmaker">deep-lying playmaker</a> in his career. Known for his vision, passing, creativity, crossing and <a href="/wiki/Set_piece_(football)" title="Set piece (football)">set-piece</a> ability,<sup id="cite_ref-Wilson_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wilson-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Scholes_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scholes-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Kroos is widely regarded as one of the best midfielders in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kroos began his senior club career playing for <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>, where he made his debut at age 17 in 2007. He was sparingly used, and opted for an 18-month loan spell at fellow <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> side <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a>, where he became a key contributor, and returned to his parent club with an increased profile in 2010. With Bayern, Kroos won two consecutive league titles, a <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Champions_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2012–13 Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> title, two <a href="/wiki/DFB-Pokal" title="DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a> titles, and was voted into the league team of the season three times. In 2014, he joined Real Madrid in a <a href="/wiki/Transfer_(association_football)" title="Transfer (association football)">transfer</a> worth €25&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Madrid, Kroos won nine trophies, including two La Liga titles and three UEFA Champions League titles, which he won consecutively from 2016 and 2018, each time being selected in the competition's team of the season. He has been selected in the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_Men&#39;s_World11" title="FIFPro">FIFPro World11</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> three times, and the league's team of the season twice.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He was voted the <a href="/wiki/IFFHS_World%27s_Best_Playmaker" class="mw-redirect" title="IFFHS World&#39;s Best Playmaker">IFFHS World's Best Playmaker</a> in 2014 and <a href="/wiki/Footballer_of_the_Year_(Germany)" title="Footballer of the Year (Germany)">German Footballer of the Year</a> in 2018.
</p><p>Kroos won Golden Player at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Under-17_Championship" title="UEFA European Under-17 Championship">2006 UEFA European Under-17 Championship</a>, where he also finished as top goalscorer, and won the Golden Ball at the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="FIFA U-17 World Cup">2007 FIFA U-17 World Cup</a>. He made his senior debut for Germany in 2010, at age 20, and appeared in five major tournaments. Kroos helped Germany win the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>, where he was top assist provider and voted to the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_All-Star_Team" class="mw-redirect" title="FIFA World Cup All-Star Team">All-Star Team</a>, <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Dream_Team" title="2014 FIFA World Cup awards">Dream Team</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team#Player_of_the_Year" title="Germany national football team">German Player of the Year</a>. At <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>, he was selected to the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship_Teams_of_the_Tournament#France_2016" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA European Championship Teams of the Tournament">Team of the Tournament</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kroos first played for local club <a href="/wiki/Greifswalder_SC" title="Greifswalder SC">Greifswalder SC</a>, later transferring to the youth team of <a href="/wiki/F.C._Hansa_Rostock" class="mw-redirect" title="F.C. Hansa Rostock">Hansa Rostock</a>. Kroos moved to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Bayern_Munich_Junior_Team" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayern Munich Junior Team">youth setup</a> in 2006. Kroos was missing up to 40 days during the school year due to training.<sup id="cite_ref-Kroosyouth_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kroosyouth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>For the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2007–08 FC Bayern Munich season">2007–08 season</a>, at the age of 17, Kroos was promoted to Bayern's senior team. He made an astounding start to his <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> career, making his debut for Bayern on 26 September 2007 in a 5–0 defeat of <a href="/wiki/FC_Energie_Cottbus" title="FC Energie Cottbus">Energie Cottbus</a> and twice <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assisting</a> <a href="/wiki/Miroslav_Klose" title="Miroslav Klose">Miroslav Klose</a> goals within 18 minutes of his appearance as a substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-hitzfeldsreview_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-hitzfeldsreview-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> At the time of his debut, Kroos was the youngest player ever to represent Bayern in a professional match at 17&#160;years, 265&#160;days old, a record since broken by <a href="/wiki/David_Alaba" title="David Alaba">David Alaba</a> in 2010.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 25 October, Kroos earned Bayern a valuable victory away to <a href="/wiki/Red_Star_Belgrade" title="Red Star Belgrade">Red Star Belgrade</a> on his <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_UEFA_Cup" title="2007–08 UEFA Cup">UEFA Cup</a> debut, coming on as a substitute in the 81st minute and providing an assist for Miroslav Klose and then scoring the winning goal, his first for the club, in stoppage time.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He made his first start for the club in a 3–1 defeat away at <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Kroos ended his first season with 20 appearances for Bayern, including six starts. He also scored three goals in 12 appearances for <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich_II" title="FC Bayern Munich II">Bayern Munich II</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Regionalliga#South" title="2007–08 Regionalliga">Regionalliga Süd</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Despite being selected to start in Bayern's opening <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Bundesliga" title="2008–09 Bundesliga">2008–09 Bundesliga</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>, Kroos appeared less frequently for <i>die Roten</i> during the first half of the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2008–09 FC Bayern Munich season">2008–09 season</a>. On 5 November 2008, however, he made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut as a 79th-minute substitute against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a> in matchday four of the <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2008–09 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loan_at_Bayer_Leverkusen">Loan at Bayer Leverkusen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Loan at Bayer Leverkusen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 31 January 2009, Bayern allowed Kroos to join <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> on an 18-month <a href="/wiki/Loan_(sports)" title="Loan (sports)">loan</a> to gain first team experience.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut on 28 February as a substitute in a 1–0 defeat against <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a>. On 12 April, he made his first Bundesliga start for Leverkusen, assisting the team's goal in a 1–1 draw with <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a>. On 18 April 2009, he scored his first Bundesliga goal in a 2–1 loss to <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">VfL Wolfsburg</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>On 30 May, Kroos appeared as a late substitute in the <a href="/wiki/2009_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2009 DFB-Pokal Final">2009 DFB-Pokal Final</a> against Werder Bremen, where Leverkusen were beaten 1–0 by a <a href="/wiki/Mesut_%C3%96zil" title="Mesut Özil">Mesut Özil</a> goal.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the 2008–09 season, Kroos made 13 appearances for Leverkusen in all competitions, scoring once.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Kroos established himself as a regular in the Leverkusen team in 2009–10, appearing all but one of Bayer's <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Bayer_04_Leverkusen_season" title="2009–10 Bayer 04 Leverkusen season">Bundesliga</a> matches. Between matchdays 16 and 20, Kroos registered five goals and four assists in five Bundesliga matches, earning him back-to-back "player of the month" awards from <a href="/wiki/Kicker_(sports_magazine)" title="Kicker (sports magazine)"><i>kicker</i></a> for December 2009 and January 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He ended the season with nine goals and 12 assists from 33 matches.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bayern_Munich">Bayern Munich</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Bayern Munich">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the summer of 2010, on the expiration of his loan at Bayer Leverkusen, Kroos returned to Bayern Munich. When asked about his first team chances with Bayern, runner-up in the previous season's <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2009–10 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, Kroos stated, "I want to play as often as possible!"<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 August 2010, he started against <a href="/wiki/TSV_Germania_Windeck" title="TSV Germania Windeck">Germania Windeck</a> in the first round of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_DFB-Pokal" title="2010–11 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a>, scoring the third goal in a 4–0 victory. On 29 October 2010, he scored his first league goal for the club, in a 4–1 win for the Bavarians against <a href="/wiki/SC_Freiburg" title="SC Freiburg">SC Freiburg</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2010–11 FC Bayern Munich season">2010–11 season</a>, Kroos was a regular starter for Bayern in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Bundesliga" title="2010–11 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a>, DFB-Pokal and <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>. He ended the season with 37 appearances in all competitions.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>During <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2011–12 FC Bayern Munich season">2011–12</a>, under <a href="/wiki/Jupp_Heynckes" title="Jupp Heynckes">Jupp Heynckes</a>, his former coach at Leverkusen, Kroos established himself as a first choice player from Bayern, forming a strong midfield partnership with <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">national team</a> colleague <a href="/wiki/Bastian_Schweinsteiger" title="Bastian Schweinsteiger">Bastian Schweinsteiger</a>. He played 51 matches in all competitions during the season, including the <a href="/wiki/2012_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2012 UEFA Champions League Final">2012 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, where Bayern were beaten on <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout" title="Penalty shootout">penalties</a> by <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Allianz_Arena" title="Allianz Arena">Allianz Arena</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Kroos was an important member of Bayern's <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a>-winning team during the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2012–13 FC Bayern Munich season">2012–13 season</a>. As the most advanced member of a midfield containing Schweinsteiger and <a href="/wiki/Javi_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="Javi Martínez">Javi Martínez</a>, Kroos scored three goals in the team's opening four <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Bundesliga" title="2012–13 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> matches. He also scored his first Champions League goal in Bayern's opening <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League group stage">group</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>. After sustaining an injury in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> quarter-final against <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Kroos was unavailable for the remainder of the season, missing Bayern's successes in the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2013 UEFA Champions League Final">2013 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2013_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2013 DFB-Pokal Final">2013 DFB-Pokal Final</a> and the last seven matches of the Bundesliga season.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Kroos returned to fitness for the start of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_FC_Bayern_Munich_season" title="2013–14 FC Bayern Munich season">2013–14 season</a> and, played in the <a href="/wiki/2013_DFL-Supercup" title="2013 DFL-Supercup">German Super Cup</a><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/2013_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2013 UEFA Super Cup">UEFA Super Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 4 October 2013, scored his first goal of the season in a 1–1 draw against former club Bayer Leverkusen in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Bundesliga" title="2013–14 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a>. He started two matches for Bayern in the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Club World Cup">2013 FIFA Club World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Toni_Kroos_»_Club_matches_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toni_Kroos_»_Club_matches-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> The first against <a href="/wiki/Guangzhou_Evergrande_Taobao_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Guangzhou Evergrande Taobao F.C.">Guangzhou Evergrande</a> in the 3–0 semi-final win on 17 December 2013,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and in the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2013 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a> as the team beat <a href="/wiki/Raja_Casablanca" class="mw-redirect" title="Raja Casablanca">Raja Casablanca</a> 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 February 2014, Kroos scored his second goal of the season in a 2–0 <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> On 25 March, he scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Hertha_BSC" title="Hertha BSC">Hertha BSC</a> as Bayern were confirmed as Bundesliga champions.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Real Madrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315:_Debut_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15:_Debut_season">2014–15: Debut season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2014–15: Debut season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1736" data-file-height="2660" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Toni_Kroos_-_CdR_-_RM_v_ATL_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kroos playing for Real Madrid in 2015</div></div></div>
<p>Prior to joining Real Madrid, Kroos had a deal in place to join <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> after agreeing terms with <a href="/wiki/David_Moyes" title="David Moyes">David Moyes</a>. However, after Moyes was sacked and <a href="/wiki/Louis_van_Gaal" title="Louis van Gaal">Louis van Gaal</a> replaced him, the Dutch manager decided against signing Kroos. Around the time of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a> he received a call from Carlo Ancelotti.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 July 2014, <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> announced that they had reached an agreement for the transfer of Kroos, signing a six-year deal for an undisclosed fee.<sup id="cite_ref-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Toni_Kroos_leaves_Bayern_Munich_for_Real_Madrid_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toni_Kroos_leaves_Bayern_Munich_for_Real_Madrid-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Toni_Kroos_joins_Real_Madrid_from_Bayern_Munich_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toni_Kroos_joins_Real_Madrid_from_Bayern_Munich-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> The press reported that Kroos had cost between €24 and €30&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Toni_Kroos_leaves_Bayern_Munich_for_Real_Madrid_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toni_Kroos_leaves_Bayern_Munich_for_Real_Madrid-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Greifswalder_SV_04" title="Greifswalder SV 04">Greifswalder SV 04</a>, the successor to his first youth team, received €60,000 from the transfer.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kroos became the ninth German player, after <a href="/wiki/G%C3%BCnter_Netzer" title="Günter Netzer">Günter Netzer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Breitner" title="Paul Breitner">Paul Breitner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uli_Stielike" title="Uli Stielike">Uli Stielike</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bernd_Schuster" title="Bernd Schuster">Bernd Schuster</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bodo_Illgner" title="Bodo Illgner">Bodo Illgner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Christoph_Metzelder" title="Christoph Metzelder">Christoph Metzelder</a>, Mesut Özil, and <a href="/wiki/Sami_Khedira" title="Sami Khedira">Sami Khedira</a>, to join Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> At his presentation in front of 8,000 supporters, he stated how Real Madrid is the "biggest club in the world" and is a "cut above Bayern".<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He played in his debut match against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014_UEFA_Super_Cup" title="2014 UEFA Super Cup">2014 UEFA Super Cup</a> on 12 August 2014, winning his first trophy at Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was part of a midfield trio with <a href="/wiki/James_Rodr%C3%ADguez" title="James Rodríguez">James Rodríguez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luka_Modri%C4%87" title="Luka Modri">Luka Modri</a> that led Real Madrid to 22-game winning run late in the year. On 8 November, Kroos scored his first goal for Real Madrid in a 5–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Rayo_Vallecano" title="Rayo Vallecano">Rayo Vallecano</a>, at home.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> In December, he helped the team win the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA Club World Cup">2014 FIFA Club World Cup</a>, leading the tournament in assists. He was named to the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro_World_XI" class="mw-redirect" title="FIFPro World XI">FIFPro World XI</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9320:_Sustained_domestic_and_European_success"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–20:_Sustained_domestic_and_European_success">2015–20: Sustained domestic and European success</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2015–20: Sustained domestic and European success">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In 2015, Ancelotti was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Rafa_Ben%C3%ADtez" class="mw-redirect" title="Rafa Benítez">Rafa Benítez</a> in Madrid's command. Benítez was replaced in the middle of the season by <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, under whom Kroos continued to be a key midfield player. Zidane said "We signed Toni because we want him to mark an era" and called Kroos "perfect for Madrid".<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> He was a regular starter when the team won the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 Champions League</a>, his second Champions League trophy.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> <i>Los Blancos'</i> triumph at <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a> meant that Kroos became the first-ever German to lift the Champions League trophy with two clubs.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 October 2016, he signed a new contract until 2022, and by the end of the year he was once again nominated to the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro_World_XI" class="mw-redirect" title="FIFPro World XI">FIFPro World XI</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> He scored the winning goal for Real Madrid in the 81-minute of the game against <a href="/wiki/RC_Celta_de_Vigo" title="RC Celta de Vigo">Celta Vigo</a> as Real Madrid won their first home game of the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> season by 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was a regular starter when Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_La_Liga" title="2016–17 La Liga">2016–17 La Liga</a> and later defended their title in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League">2016–17 Champions League</a>. He became the first German player to win the trophy three times.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> During the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 UEFA Champions League</a>, he made twelve appearances, when Madrid won their third consecutive and 13th overall Champions League title.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 December 2018, Kroos won his record fifth <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="FIFA Club World Cup">FIFA Club World Cup</a> after his team defeated <a href="/wiki/Al_Ain_FC" title="Al Ain FC">Al Ain FC</a> with a 4–1 margin in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_Club_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA Club World Cup Final">final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On 20 May 2019, he extended his contract with the club until 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> On 12 January 2020, Kroos won the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2019–20 Supercopa de España">2019–20 Supercopa de España</a> with Real Madrid beating the local rivals <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He was a regular starter during the league season, scoring four goals, as Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_La_Liga" title="2019–20 La Liga">2019–20 La Liga</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG/170px-FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG" decoding="async" width="170" height="174" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG/255px-FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/36/FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG/340px-FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG 2x" data-file-width="1584" data-file-height="1623" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:FIFA_WC-qualification_2014_-_Austria_vs._Germany_2012-09-11_-_Toni_Kroos.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kroos with Germany in 2012</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_teams">Youth teams</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Youth teams">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2007_FIFA_U-17_World_Cup" title="2007 FIFA U-17 World Cup">2007 FIFA U-17 World Cup</a>, Toni Kroos was awarded the Golden Ball as the tournament's best player and also won the <i>Bronze Shoe</i> after scoring five goals.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Kroos' debut for the <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_under-21_football_team" title="Germany national under-21 football team">national U-21 team</a> came on 5 September 2008 in a <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-21_Football_Championship_Qualification_Group_9" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-21 Football Championship Qualification Group 9">2009 Euro U-21 Championship Qualifier</a> against <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland_national_under-21_football_team" title="Northern Ireland national under-21 football team">Northern Ireland</a> and scored the opening goal in the 11th minute,<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> his second goal for the U-21 side was goal in Germany's 1–0 win over Italy, a precise long-range shot in the angle. It came as a surprise that coach <a href="/wiki/Horst_Hrubesch" title="Horst Hrubesch">Horst Hrubesch</a> left him out of Germany's U-21 squad for <a href="/wiki/2009_UEFA_European_Under-21_Football_Championship" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 UEFA European Under-21 Football Championship">Euro 2009</a>, and Germany went on to win the tournament without him.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_World_Cup">2010 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2010 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In January 2010, Kroos was called up to the senior <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> team for the first time, for a training session in <a href="/wiki/Sindelfingen" title="Sindelfingen">Sindelfingen</a><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> and was named in the squad for the following match, a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> on 3 March 2010, in which he subsequently made his debut for the national side.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kroos was selected to <a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a>'s <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#Germany" title="2010 FIFA World Cup squads">23-man squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> in South Africa. He made his <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> debut in Germany's final group-stage match versus <a href="/wiki/Ghana_national_football_team" title="Ghana national football team">Ghana</a>, coming on in the 80th minute for Bastian Schweinsteiger, with Germany leading 1–0. He made further appearances as a substitute in the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Argentina_vs_Germany" title="2010 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">quarter-finals</a> against Argentina, in the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Germany_vs_Spain" title="2010 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">semi-finals</a> against <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> and in the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Third_place_play-off" title="2010 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">third place play-off</a> against <a href="/wiki/Uruguay_national_football_team" title="Uruguay national football team">Uruguay</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2012">Euro 2012</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Euro 2012">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:232px;"><a href="/wiki/File:UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_(06).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg/230px-UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="230" height="153" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg/345px-UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg/460px-UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_%2806%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1800" data-file-height="1200" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_-_Austria_vs_Germany_2011-06-03_(06).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kroos (left) battles <a href="/wiki/Julian_Baumgartlinger" title="Julian Baumgartlinger">Julian Baumgartlinger</a> for the ball in a <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a> in <a href="/wiki/Vienna" title="Vienna">Vienna</a> (<a href="/wiki/Ernst-Happel-Stadion" title="Ernst-Happel-Stadion">Ernst-Happel-Stadion</a>).</div></div></div>
<p>Kroos established himself as a regular starter in Germany's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">qualification</a> campaign for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>, playing in eight out of a possible ten games. Germany won all ten qualifying matches to top <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_Group_A" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying Group A">group A</a>. After qualification was already ensured, Kroos scored his first two international goals, both with his strong right foot. Notably, both Kroos' goals were Germany's first after falling behind in the respective matches, both of which were drawn away friendlies, against the two Euro 2012 hosts – <a href="/wiki/Poland_national_football_team" title="Poland national football team">Poland</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a>. National coach <a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a> also praised him: "How Toni distributes the ball, how he receives it, is very good. He's technically excellent ... He has made progress in the last few matches, I'm extremely satisfied with the player."<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the tournament finals, Kroos appeared as a substitute in all three of Germany's <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Group_B" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Group B">Group B</a> matches. For the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_knockout_stage#Germany_vs_Italy" class="mw-redirect" title="UEFA Euro 2012 knockout stage">semi-final</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, Löw selected the naturally attacking Kroos to <a href="/wiki/Marking_(association_football)" title="Marking (association football)">man mark</a> Italy's <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a> <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a>. The decision was heavily criticised as Germany lost the match 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup">2014 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2014 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>During Germany's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_C" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group C">2014 World Cup qualifying campaign</a>, Kroos scored his first two competitive international goals in a 6–1 win over the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Dublin" title="Dublin">Dublin</a>. On 6 September 2013, he scored the team's second goal in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Kroos was named in Germany's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> In the team's opening match, a 4–0 defeat of <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a>, Kroos started in midfield and assisted <a href="/wiki/Mats_Hummels" title="Mats Hummels">Mats Hummels</a> for Germany's second goal.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Then in the quarter final the only goal scored by <a href="/wiki/Mats_Hummels" title="Mats Hummels">Mats Hummels</a> against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> came from his free kick.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Semi-finals" title="2014 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">semi-final</a> against the host nation <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>, Kroos scored two goals two minutes apart (24' and 26') in Germany's <a href="/wiki/Brazil_v_Germany_(2014_FIFA_World_Cup)" title="Brazil v Germany (2014 FIFA World Cup)">7–1 win</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He also recorded his fourth assist of the tournament, crossing for <a href="/wiki/Thomas_M%C3%BCller" title="Thomas Müller">Thomas Müller</a>'s opening goal, and was named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a> by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Kroos has been nicknamed <i>Garçom</i> ("waiter" in Portuguese) by the Brazilians for precisely delivering most passes to the strikers.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 July, Kroos was named on the ten-man shortlist for FIFA's <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Golden_Ball" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">Golden Ball</a> award for the tournament's best player.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Castrol_Performance_Index" class="mw-redirect" title="Castrol Performance Index">Castrol Performance Index</a>, the official statistical analyser of the World Cup, rated Kroos as the best player at the 2014 World Cup, with a rating of 9.79 out of 10.<sup id="cite_ref-castrol_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-castrol-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kroos is considered the only player from the former <a href="/wiki/East_Germany" title="East Germany">German Democratic Republic</a> to ever win the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 4 June 2018, Kroos was included in Germany's final 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 23 June, Kroos scored from a free-kick in stoppage time against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a> to resurrect Germany's World Cup hopes with a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> But in their next and last group stage match, his side were knocked out by <a href="/wiki/South_Korea_national_football_team" title="South Korea national football team">South Korea</a> after losing 2–0 four days later.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_UEFA_Nations_League"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_UEFA_Nations_League">2020–21 UEFA Nations League</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2020–21 UEFA Nations League">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 13 October 2020, Kroos played his 100th match for Germany in a 3–3 draw against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Nations_League_A" title="2020–21 UEFA Nations League A">2020–21 UEFA Nations League A</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:20%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"How Toni distributes the ball, how he receives it, is very good. He's technically excellent ... He has made progress in the last few matches, I'm extremely satisfied with the player."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">–<a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a>, Manager of the Germany National Football Team<sup id="cite_ref-goal.com2012-04-18_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal.com2012-04-18-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>A tall and athletic right-footed midfielder, Kroos is known for the range and accuracy of his distribution with either foot, his technique, vision, creativity, reading of the game, and his ability to dictate play in midfield or set up goals with his passing and ball delivery from <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">set-pieces</a>; he is also capable of scoring goals himself, courtesy of his striking ability – in particular from long range – and his accuracy from free kicks.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> He has been described by <a href="/wiki/Jonathan_Wilson_(writer)" title="Jonathan Wilson (writer)">Jonathan Wilson</a> as "perhaps the archetype of the modern <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Attacking_midfielder" title="Midfielder">attacking midfielder</a>". Wilson has also described Kroos as "dynamic and hardworking", and has praised him for his versatility, physical strength and ability to play in several <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfield</a> positions: in addition to his usual role, he has also been used in the centre as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deep-lying</a> <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">playmaker</a>, on the <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">flank</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Box-to-box_midfielder" title="Midfielder">box-to-box role</a>, or even as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive midfielder</a>, due to his ability to both break up play, retain possession, and create chances for teammates.<sup id="cite_ref-Wilson_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Wilson-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> Former <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> midfielder <a href="/wiki/Paul_Scholes" title="Paul Scholes">Paul Scholes</a> said in 2014 that Kroos, "a top-class <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central midfielder</a>", was the player that United most needed to sign.<sup id="cite_ref-Scholes_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Scholes-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Former <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> captain <a href="/wiki/Johan_Cruyff" title="Johan Cruyff">Johan Cruyff</a> said of Kroos' performances at the 2014 World Cup, "He's doing everything right: the pace in his passes is great and he sees everything. It's nearly perfect."<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kroos was born in <a href="/wiki/Greifswald" title="Greifswald">Greifswald</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mecklenburg-Vorpommern" title="Mecklenburg-Vorpommern">Mecklenburg-Vorpommern</a>, on 4 January 1990.<sup id="cite_ref-Toni_Kroos_joins_Real_Madrid_from_Bayern_Munich_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Toni_Kroos_joins_Real_Madrid_from_Bayern_Munich-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He has a younger brother, <a href="/wiki/Felix_Kroos" title="Felix Kroos">Felix Kroos</a>, who is also a professional footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-Kroosyouth_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kroosyouth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> His father Roland works as youth coach for Hansa Rostock.<sup id="cite_ref-Kroosyouth_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kroosyouth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During his youth, he was a mediocre student and spent a lot of time practising football,<sup id="cite_ref-Kroosyouth_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kroosyouth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> however, he was well-behaved in class and well liked among his peers at school.<sup id="cite_ref-Kroosyouth_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kroosyouth-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kroos married his long-term girlfriend Jessica Farber on 13 June 2015. They have two sons, Leon (born 14 August 2013),<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Fin (born 26 March 2019)<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> and daughter, Amelie (born on 20 July 2016).<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> He owns a house on the island of <a href="/wiki/Mallorca" title="Mallorca">Mallorca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Vertrag_bis_2020!_Kroos_wechselt_zu_Real_Madrid-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Toni_Kroos&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
